 He is also considered an expert in these subjects
 in deshon ke sahitya, raajnneeti, parivesh or bauddhik hulchalon par unhone paryaapt vimarsh or niyamit lekhan kiya he

 prabud-samvedansheel srujak kii drushti or uski purvaagrah rahit mudra ke kaaran sharma ne bhartiya samaaj main alpsankhyakon kii samasyaon or unke samaadhaan bhi sujhaaye hai

 sharma saamaajik vishmataaon ko dainandin ghatnaon or apane aasapaas ke paatro ke madhyam se ubhaarne main paarangat hai

 unke saat upanyaas or lagbhag 130 kahaniyon ke kai sanskaran prakashit ho chuke hai
 All his published stories are present in this compilation in three volumes
 apni shuruaati kahaniyon main sharma ne ek aisa prakhar stri-vivek or vimarsh kiya jisamen badbolapan nahin he balki vishisht stri-bhashaa ke nazariye se bhi unke yogadan ko rekhaankit kiya ja saktaa he

 sharma ek satark stri kii aankh se apane samay or samaaj main apni pahchaan ke liye jujhne vaali auraton kii ladaai or himmat ko dekhati or vyakt karti hai
 Sharma has examined human relations in the context of time and society
 unhone yah sab prastaavit kiya he ki samaaj kahin kaa bhi ho, usamen jivit log pehle apane astitv ke liye sangharsh karte hai or phir bade insaani sarokaaron ko bachaane ke liye ladate hai
